Hana Maru Liner Suspends Service in Shanghai, Shanghai-Dinghai and Ningbo-Dinghai Routes Resume Smoothly 70

After the resumption of the Shanghai-Ningbo route, there were problems with the Shanghai-Dinghai route, but the Ningbo-Dinghai route has been successfully resumed. A Datong News Agency reporter recorded the actual situation as follows:

Shanghai-Ningbo Route

After the Lihe Shipping Department's Moufu Wheel successfully sailed from Shanghai to Ningbo the day before yesterday, the Sino-Italian Consalia Wheel was originally scheduled to sail to Ningbo yesterday. However, due to the bombing of Ningbo, stevedores loading and unloading goods at the dock have to return to the city to work at night, so the wheel was rescheduled to depart at 4:00 AM this morning, arriving in Ningbo by evening. The Deping Wheel has departed from Wenzhou and is en route to Shanghai, arriving today and departing for Ningbo tomorrow. If time is not sufficient, it will be postponed to the morning of the 24th.

Ningbo-Dinghai Route

After the Far East Hana Maru Liner and the Lu Lin Gaodeng Wheel successively sailed to Dinghai on the 19th, both wheels arrived in Dinghai on the morning of the 20th. The Hana Maru Liner left Dinghai at 4:00 PM yesterday, carrying passengers and cargo, and is expected to arrive in Shanghai at 8:00 AM today. The Gaodeng Wheel stayed in Dinghai for one day, and resumed service to Ningbo for the first time at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. The journey was very smooth, and the ship arrived safely in Ningbo at 2:00 PM. The wheel is scheduled to depart from Ningbo to Dinghai again today, and will routinely operate on the Ningbo-Dinghai route from now on.

Shanghai-Dinghai Route

According to information received by the Datong News Agency reporter, the Hana Maru Liner will temporarily suspend service on the Shanghai-Dinghai route after returning to Shanghai from Dinghai. It is likely to be reassigned to Wenzhou. The wheel's authorities have not provided a reason for the suspension. Therefore, the resumption of shipping to Shanghai-Dinghai has been short lived and will apparently be suspended again. It is also rumored that the Taikoo New Beijing Wheel will sail to Ningbo today, but this is inaccurate, as the wheel is currently in Tianjin.

Spring Cocoons Begin to Enter the Market, Shanghai Merchants Purchase Separately, Zhejiang Native Cocoons Suffer Poor Harvest, Estimated to Be About 30% Lower, Jiangzhe Improved Cocoons Expected to Be Better 71

Spring cocoons from Jiangsu and Zhejiang have begun to enter the market. Cities within the occupied areas are controlled by the "Central China Company," while individual silk factories in Shanghai are free to purchase cocoons from various townships. Zhejiang native cocoons have suffered a poor harvest this year. Improved cocoons are about to enter the scene and are expected to be better. Shanghai factories will resume operations as soon as the new cocoons arrive. Details are as follows:

Shanghai Merchants Allowed to Purchase Cocoons in Townships

The "Central China Silk Company" originally intended to control the spring cocoons in the occupied areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, prohibiting Shanghai silk factories from purchasing them. However, due to the guerrillas destroying the cocoon shops everywhere, the Company, realizing the difficulty of controlling cocoon shops in townships, and after strenuous efforts by Shanghai silk factories, agreed to abandon the control of cocoon shops in townships, allowing Shanghai factories to purchase freely. Shanghai factories are now going to various townships to set up shops for purchase, and have prepared certificates from the Shanghai Silk Manufacturers' Association. However, the cocoons purchased must be taxed to the "Renovation Government" before they are allowed to be transported to Shanghai.

Poor Native Harvest, Improved Cocoons are Still Good

Native cocoons from Hangzhou, Haining, Jiaxing, Deqing, and other counties in Zhejiang have been put on the market. The price in Hangzhou is 42 yuan (national currency) per dan (18 tael balance). The price of the best native cocoons in Changan, Haining is 45 yuan (national currency) per dan. However, due to weather conditions, the harvest of native cocoons in various counties of Zhejiang Province this year has been about 30% lower. As for the improved varieties, they will soon enter the scene and are expected to have a better harvest. Because the weather has been very good in recent days, it is suitable for improved varieties to form cocoons. It is said that improved varieties in Wuxi, Suzhou, Changzhou, Danyang, and other places in Jiangsu are scheduled to appear on the market at the end of this month or early next month.

Shanghai Factories Waiting for Cocoons to Start Operations

There are approximately 45 silk factories in the Shanghai concession. Due to the lack of raw materials, they have been forced to stop work one after another. As of yesterday, only a few factories, such as Jardine, were barely maintaining operations. Regarding the purchase of cocoons from the occupied areas this year, although silver shops have stopped lending tortoise money and insurance companies have stopped insuring various risks, in order to avoid running out of raw materials, they still risk buying from the occupied areas. It has now been decided that operations will resume as soon as the new cocoons arrive in Shanghai, and it has been decided that day and night shifts will be worked to rush the silk reeling. It is expected that after the spring cocoons are put on the market, the number of silk factories in Shanghai will increase to more than 50.

Spring Cocoons from Eastern Zhejiang Approved for Shipment to Shanghai

Shaoxing, Xiaoshan, Xinchang, Shengxian, Zhuji, and other counties in eastern Zhejiang are also the only cocoon-producing areas. They have now been fully put on the market and purchased by local factories and remaining cocoon merchants. The Zhejiang Provincial Local Bank and the Camellia Oil and Silk Management Office have allocated 1.5 million yuan to handle spring cocoon loans. It is said that the cocoons produced in the above counties are all native varieties. As for improved varieties, they are rarely hatched. The harvest this year is better than that in western Zhejiang. The Trade Commission originally intended to control their transportation and sale, but at the request of Shanghai factories, it has agreed to allow them to be transported to Shanghai by wheel from Ningbo.

Small-Scale Silk Industry Forced to Close, Silk Raw Materials Under Control, Prices Increase by 10-20% 72

There are no less than 300 to 400 large and small electric weaving silk factories in this city. According to sources in the silk industry, due to the control of silk-producing areas, raw materials are scarce in Shanghai, resulting in a daily decrease in inventory and an increase in selling prices. Except for most small-scale electric factories in western Shanghai, which are limited by capital and unable to operate, and are forced to close, the prices of various silk fabrics produced by major electric weaving silk factories have increased by 10-20% due to the high cost of raw materials. As for sales to other ports, Yunnan, Guiyang, Sichuan, Kunming, and other places are the main destinations, but due to the high cost of shipping, the profits are quite low.

Concession Authorities Strictly Investigate Rice Market Manipulation, Dispatch Personnel to Stations Every Morning for Investigation, Rice Industry Still Enforces Price Limits 73

Since the Rice Grain Evaluation Committee, due to the difficulty of its work, resolved to dissolve itself voluntarily, yesterday morning, the rice market transactions changed from private to public prices. In addition to finding ways to dredge sources of origin, the Bean and Rice Industry Association still maintained its previous stance on the issue of price limits and strictly enforced them. The concession authorities are determined to severely crack down on hoarding households for speculation and manipulation and will punish them. Grain firms that handle entrepot grain secretly ordered foreign rice. Details of each situation are recorded as follows:

Private Trade Becomes Public Market Price

The Shanghai rice industry market has been manipulated by speculators with financial resources, resulting in a sharp rise in market prices. In addition to the 15 yuan price limit, private trading has increased by 2 to 3 yuan. Only because the buying and selling parties secretly transact, enforcement is very difficult, and the work of the evaluation committee has been severely hindered, so it was resolved to dissolve it. After the market opened at 9:00 AM yesterday morning, the buying and selling parties were like drunkards, trading in large quantities at the original private market price, which has changed to open bidding. The highest white rice price in the first half of the market rose to 18.12 yuan, while in the second half of the market, it fell slightly, but its highest market price was still between 17.78 yuan and 18 yuan. General hoarding households, seeing the increase in sales, again stopped selling high- and medium-grade japonica rice, hoarding and raising prices.

Rice Price Limit Not Revoked

Since the Evaluation Committee resolved to dissolve itself on the 20th of this month, some simple-minded rice merchants believed that the price limit had been revoked along with it, so they acted wantonly in the market, becoming even more unrestrained and transacting on a large scale. According to investigations by the Dagang News Agency, the rice price limit was decided by the seven rice industry groups in the city at the third joint meeting. The Rice Grain Evaluation Committee was also produced by these groups. Although the Evaluation Committee has been dissolved, the case of the rice price limit still exists and has not been revoked. In terms of law, the Evaluation Committee should not have decided to dissolve itself. According to precedent, the power of dissolution must be decided by the seven groups to be legal.

Concession Authorities Crack Down on Manipulation

The Public Works Bureau of the Public Concession and the Municipal Council of the French Concession are extremely concerned about the regulation of rice grain and the high prices in Shanghai. Detailed investigations have been made into various grains that are directly related to people's food, and it is believed that the existing stocks of rice and flour in Shanghai are sufficient to maintain supply for six months, and there is no shortage even during the lean season. The current abnormal surge in market prices in the rice market, increasing the burden on citizens and affecting public order, is extremely serious. It is evident that speculators are manipulating the market, which is abhorrent. Therefore, the two authorities have already ordered the police to dispatch detectives to the market every morning for secret investigations. Once discovered, they will be severely cracked down and severely punished as a warning to others.

Ways to Dredge Sources of Rice Grain

The registration of rice stocks by owners, which was organized by the previous Price Committee, will end in a few days. Regarding the investigation of rice stocks in the two concessions of Shanghai thereafter, it has been decided that the Bean and Rice Industry Association will be responsible for continuing to handle it. Although dredging the source of national rice is beyond the power of rice industry groups, in order to maintain the people's food in the concession, it has been decided to make every effort to ensure that the people's food is not in panic. Rice merchants have all taken maintaining the people's food and taking care of the overall situation as their purpose, and are making every effort to dredge sources, and will not take profit as the only goal. According to the current situation forecast, the rice and grain situation in Shanghai will not reach a very serious level, and the situation in the winter of 1937 will not be repeated.

Secretly Entrusted to Order Foreign Rice

According to investigations by the Dagang News Agency, recently, some rice and grain companies that specialize in entrepot trade, seeing that the price of national rice has soared and is equal to the price of foreign rice, and that it is continuing to rise, have ordered foreign rice from Saigon, Annam, and other places abroad, all entrusted to foreign firms to handle. However, the orderers are keeping it a secret, and the amount is about 10,000 to 100,000 bags. As for the foreign rice that has been imported from January to March this year, the total amount is 700,912.9 metric tons, valued at 12,232,638 yuan (national currency).

Shanghai Telephone Company Business Report 1938 74

According to the Shanghai Telephone Company's report for the year ended December 31, 1938, in terms of economic income, its profit was 948,200 yuan (Chinese currency), which was 20,205 yuan more than in 1917. Although its net income was better than in the previous year, various operating expenses have also increased compared to the previous year. At the beginning of 1938, the telephone business showed a vigorous atmosphere, and the number of people who needed telephone service was increasing day by day. Therefore, after the year-end statistics, the number of telephones exceeded the highest number before the war by 2,966. In the year 1938, the number of telephones increased by 17,860. As of December 31, 1938, the total number of telephones was 62,355.

In addition to the significant increase in the number of telephones, the number of uses per telephone has also increased. In 1938, the total number of calls made was 126 million, which was 24 million more than the number in 19317, which was 102 million. In order to cope with this rapid development, 7,000 additional meters were installed. Also, due to the increase in telephones in various new areas, additional trunk lines were added to meet the needs.

In addition, the reconstruction of the main stations that needed repair, such as Hongqiao Road and Huade Road, was also completed in 1938. In May, telephone service was restored in various areas near Shanghai. Telephone communication between Shanghai and Japan was restored in mid-October. And starting on January 1, 1939, telephone communication between Shanghai and the mainland was restored, in two locations.

French Huifeng Bank Praises the Reliability of Chinese Government Bonds 75

The French-language Shanghai Daily reported on the 21st that at the recent shareholders' meeting of the local French Huifeng Bank (transliteration), the board of directors presented a report praising the reliability of Chinese government bonds. It was stated that since the outbreak of the war, the Chinese government has been able to maintain the credibility of its domestic debt and is fully responsible for it. It is reported that the bank's operations last year generated a net profit of 167,790.87 yuan, which could have distributed a dividend of 7%, but the bank's authorities, for the sake of prudence, only distributed a dividend of 3.5%, totaling 70,000 yuan, and the remaining profit of 97,790.87 yuan was carried over to the next operating year.

Public Works Bureau Revises Cold Drink Regulations 77

Restaurants Not Allowed to Use Cold Dishes

Whether to Continue This Year is Still Under Study The Public Works Bureau's Health Department believes that with the arrival of summer and the increasingly hot weather, unclean cold drinks are likely to cause disease, so it is extremely concerned. Recently, it has revised Article 4 of the Other Food License Regulations as follows: "Soda water and non-carbonated water for human consumption shall be made with clean and sanitary water that has been boiled, distilled, filtered, or disinfected by other methods in a hygienic manner, and a new clause has been added:" Distilled water for human consumption shall be distilled with clean and sanitary water in a hygienic manner." Also, last summer, the Public Works Bureau's Health Department, due to the unhygienic nature of the cold dishes in restaurants, ordered the Restaurant Association not to use them, which was quite effective. This year's deadline is approaching, and the Bureau is currently studying whether to continue to implement it, and will issue a clear order.

Permanent Commemoration Measures for Wang Yiting According to investigations, various groups in this city have established the Wang Qinda Permanent Commemoration Committee and are actively studying it. According to sources in the Commemoration Committee, in addition to maintaining and expanding the orphanages and disability homes founded by Wang before his death, the Lake Society is also planning commemoration measures to honor Wang's methods and respect his fellow villagers. In addition, the Commemoration Committee will petition the National Government to publish Wang's life story in the National History Biography, and this petition will soon be implemented to show the State's meaning of decorating the final rites.

Chinese Guerrillas Destroy Railroad Tracks, Burn Kunshan Station, Japanese Side is Panicked and Has Implemented Vigilance, Pressurized Cars are Dispatched for Patrols from Time to Time 79

Dagang News Agency reports that since the Chinese guerrilla forces controlled the outer circle of the Jiangzhe occupied area, they have given the Japanese side significant blows from time to time. Therefore, the Japanese army along the three railway lines of Jinghu, Sujiahu, and Hangzhou did not dare to lightly transfer troops. The other day, the Shanghai-Hangzhou railway tracks were destroyed by the Chinese army. According to people from Kunshan, Kunshan Station was suddenly set on fire and burned down some time ago, and the station building was almost completely destroyed. The railway material room there was also burned down, causing considerable losses. At the same time, a section of track between Kunshan and Qingyang Port was also demolished, so the Japanese army was even more frightened. Recently, in addition to dispatching pressurized cars from time to time for patrols along the lines, stone squares were also erected on both sides of the road and painted with red paint as a warning line, prohibiting people from crossing them. People in various places are also notified to report any damage to the railway tracks. Because the Japanese side has been very busy with military transportation on the lines recently, they are deeply afraid of being attacked.

Report on Meteorological Signals, Changed to Hoisting on the French Concession Signal Tower, Moved from the Anchorage of Pilot Boats at the Mouth of the Yangtze River, Using International Language Flag Signals to Indicate Climate 80

The Port Affairs Section of the Jianghai Customs, in order to change the meteorological signals used to report the weather, which were originally hoisted at the anchorage of pilot boats at the entrance of the Yangtze River, to being hoisted on the Shanghai Observatory signal tower on the Bund of the French Concession, issued Announcement No. 2: "It is hereby decided that starting on June 1 of this year, all signals originally used to report the weather at the anchorage of pilot boats at the entrance of the Yangtze River will be changed to being hoisted daily from 11:00 AM to 11:30 AM (the observation time is 10:00 AM local time) on the Shanghai Observatory signal tower on the Bund of the French Concession. These signals all use International Language flag signals. The flag signal at the top is used to indicate the degree of wind direction (N for north, S for south, E for east, W for west). The next flag signal is used to indicate the number of wind force according to the Beaufort scale. The wind force above number 10 is not usually indicated. At that time, the Customs flag platform will already have hoisted a gale signal separately. Other signals such as the F flag signal indicate heavy fog, the U flag signal indicates not sunny, and the V flag signal indicates changing wind direction. This announcement is hereby issued to inform all wheel merchants, etc. Special announcement."

Unstable Situation in Fujian Sea, Shanghai-Fujian Shipping Disrupted, Foreign Shipping Companies Plan to Temporarily Suspend Sailings for Safety 83

The situation in the Fujian Sea has become tense due to harassment by Japanese aircraft and warships. Later, as the Japanese warships left one after another, the situation eased somewhat. However, according to recent reports received by the shipping industry, Japanese warships in the Fujian Sea are moving very frequently. On the morning of the 19th, Fuzhou was bombarded by Japanese warships, and Japanese aircraft also flew to Dabi for bombing. Currently, there are five Japanese warships anchored outside the port of Mawei, constantly launching speedboats for reconnaissance, indicating some intention. The situation is quite tense. The Shanghai-Fujian shipping routes originally included three major routes: Fuzhou, Quanzhou, and Xinghua. Since the economic center of gravity of Fujian Province shifted to Quanzhou and other places, passenger and cargo transportation has prospered. Now, various foreign shipping companies, due to the tense situation in Fujian Province and for the sake of shipping safety, plan to temporarily suspend sailings and dock in Shanghai. Therefore, shipping from Shanghai to Fujian Province may be interrupted indefinitely.

Charity Art Exhibition Closed Last Night 84

The Shanghai Art Charity Relief Exhibition, organized by the China Industrial and Commercial Art Writers Association, has been held on the fourth floor of the Great Sun Company since its opening on the twelfth of this month. The items collected, though small, are all crystallizations of art, and have been highly valued by all sectors. Divided into categories such as arts and crafts, commercial art, paintings, Western paintings, sculptures, artistic photography, antiques, etc., there were no fewer than 5,000 pieces, which were replaced daily. In particular, Wu Guangji's jade seal boxes of various styles and the finely carved sailboat models are considered top-notch. As for the truly large goose skin produced in Longxi, meticulously crafted to be soft and smooth, with jade-like purity and a lustrous sheen, priced at 1,000 yuan, it was even more a highlight of the venue. The association, with the ten-day period expired, announced its closure at 7:00 p.m. last night. This exhibition was entirely for the purpose of charity relief. Except for the exhibitors who declared that they would take back half the price, the rest was donated to refugee relief efforts.

A Youth Model Person 86

— Zhou

——Mr. Yuan Ludeng——

Mr. Yuan Ludeng is a youth model person who succeeded through hard study in his youth. In middle age, he served the society and participated in all kinds of public welfare activities. Throughout his life, he benefited from "knowing contentment and not being disgraced." His interests are quite in the style of Tao Jingjie, and even his drinking is very much in the spirit of "friends knowing he is good at drinking, they may set up wine and invite him." However, he does not necessarily aim to get drunk.

When the reporter went to interview him, Mr. Yuan was waving his hand and sending off the processing of his official duties at the Refugee Association. He is sixty-one years old this year, and his spirit is vigorous. A cloth gown clearly shows his simple habits. Behind his seat hangs a picture of a white-haired man entertaining his parents, commemorating his family's four generations under one roof. Grand Historian Shen Qiquan (art) and others wrote poems for him, saying, "Joyful laughter in the hall above, laughter below, indeed filial sons and virtuous grandchildren."

We began to talk about the future of refugee relief, and he said: There are currently more than 50,000 refugees housed in the Shanghai International Settlement. Including the refugee areas in Nanshi, there should be more than 100,000. The street refugees who have not been housed, and those who have recently come to Shanghai to take refuge, are still impossible to count. Currently, donations from all sectors can be described as enthusiastic. The association is actively working on the production and education of refugees, paying particular attention to the resettlement of refugees. Within a considerable period of time, a concrete result can be expected, giving refugees the technical skills to support themselves. Of course, this concrete result still requires the continued efforts and assistance of all sectors.

He began to speak freely about his personal interests and living conditions. He said that in addition to opium, he has always been fond of both smoking and drinking. However, for more than ten years, he has not bought wine or cigarettes himself, always receiving gifts from friends. He has the style of "only wine has no limit." I asked him, "How about two catties?" He said, "Three catties are also fine." He gets up at 6:30 every morning, practices martial arts, and goes to the association at 9:00 to handle official duties. He has several self-criticisms regarding his own strengths and weaknesses in life: (1) I have been trained by missionary schools since childhood and am determined to adhere to the principle of benefiting others at the expense of oneself. I have never been troubled by any hobbies in my life. (2) I came from humble beginnings as a student, and I have never forgotten the situation at the time. No matter how smooth the circumstances, I have never aspired to be pampered and comfortable. (3) I have never been annoyed by occasional setbacks. I have always held the ancient teaching of accepting adversity with equanimity. (4) I have never harbored selfish opinions in my life, whether towards society or family. I would rather suffer sacrifices than seek my own advantage. (5) Although I have often followed the customs and trends in recent years, I have never dared to cross the boundaries of morality. As for the weaknesses of self-examination, they are: (1) I am naturally straightforward. When I see someone's faults, I must advise them, or even rebuke them in person. I may not be able to be forgiven by others. Although I want to try to cultivate patience, it is already too late. (2) In my life, I place too much emphasis on sentiment. I often act rashly regardless of my abilities, such as investing in unlimited companies and serving as a director of unregistered joint-stock companies, and providing unlimited guarantees for others. I know there is a risk of bankruptcy, but I often think that people will not deceive me, and I do not know how to warn myself. (3) I am not good at managing money. As long as I have money on hand, or have a way to raise funds, I will help others in difficulty. As a result, my own burden has become heavier and heavier, and I have to rely on the help of close friends, which makes me feel ashamed. Speaking to this point, he hopes that young people in the business community can use his self-criticism as a reference.

Continuing in his recollection, he narrated the circumstances of his hard study in his youth, saying: "When I was ten years old, I went to school with my younger brother. Three years later, because of the poverty of the family, even the meager tuition fees were difficult to raise. I originally planned to drop out of school, but at that time I wanted to learn a trade, but I suffered from the lack of someone to support me. At that time, the British Jesus Church and the Common Society happened to set up a Kai Ming School in Yong, with an attached primary school, which did not charge tuition. So I went to school there. After two more years, it was changed to Fei Di Middle School. My younger brother and I were favored by the missionaries and admitted to the school free of charge. The following year, I took the exam and was fortunate enough to win the championship. I also received an annual scholarship of six pounds sterling from the Royal Education Road School in London. The missionary distributed half of it for tuition and half for family use." At this point, Mr. Yuan has become a good young man who dared to study in a poor family. (To be continued)

Page 11

Tragedy of Fire in Guling Road, Strict Interrogation into Cause of Fire, Cook Denies That Burned Yarn Spools Caused the Fire, Paper Shop Has Fire Insurance Worthy of Note 87

In the kitchen of the Chen family at No. 70 Guling Road, a fire suddenly broke out at around 5:00 a.m. on the 11th of this month. The wind was strong, and the flames immediately shot up, burning through the mezzanine floor. Chen Zubei, a water company worker living upstairs, and his wife and children, were awakened from their dreams by the burning skin. They got up in extreme pain and immediately carried his wife, Mrs. Yu, and their seven-year-old third son, Shi Mai, jumping and escaping. Mrs. Yu suffered minor injuries. Their thirteen-year-old daughter, Jin Di, also escaped, but had been burned. The most tragic were their ten-year-old eldest son, Qingqing, and nine-year-old second son, Yu Qing, who

perished in the fire

After the fire brigade extinguished the fire, Chen Da, a detective from the New Zha Pu Fang in charge, and others arrived at the scene. They sent the injured to the hospital for treatment, examined the burnt corpses, and ordered them to be collected. It was later found that the fire was caused by the re-ignition of the ashes of burned yarn spools placed by Shi Chenglang, a Tongzhou cook hired by Qian Jichen, who was operating cotton yarn in the third room of the house. The fire spread to the paper piled nearby, causing such a tragedy. Shi was arrested and sent to the First Special District Court and prosecuted according to law. The details of the interrogation and detention have been recorded in previous reports. Now, the thirteen-year-old girl, Jin Di, who was burned, also

succumbed to her injuries

and died a few days ago. Therefore, Chen Zubei's three sons and one daughter, now only the youngest Bao Bao remains. Although Mrs. Yu's injuries have been healed, she is extremely grieved by the tragic death of her two children. On Saturday, the case was heard in the Second Criminal Court by Judge Xiao of the First Special Court. When Shi Chenglang was brought up for further interrogation, Chen Yu stood beside the case, tears streaming down her face. She also stated that the defendant usually stored the ashes from burning yarn spools in a Pu bag and had repeatedly seen him placing the Pu bag near the pile of paper. She had advised him, but the defendant never listened.

resulting in the tragedy

Chen Awu, a cooking apprentice from the second landlord Chen's family, testified that he and Shi cooked in the same stove. Shi always cooked first in the stove at five or six in the morning, while he started cooking at seven or eight. Shi always used a Pu saw to store the ashes from burning yarn spools, so that he could pick out iron pieces in his spare time and sell them. When questioned, Shi flatly denied that he had caused the fire. Then the debate began. Li Zhishan, the lawyer from the Public Security Bureau, argued that, based on the physical evidence of the burned yarn spools obtained by the Public Security Bureau and the testimony of Chen Awu, it could be proved that the defendant was responsible for the disaster and should be punished according to the law. However, Wang Xiaowen, the defendant's defense lawyer, requested the court to pay

close attention

to the fact that the second landlord of the house had set up a paper shop in the house and had fire insurance of 8,000 taels of silver. According to insurance regulations, compensation is only given if someone else's fire spreads and affects the insured. Chen Awu is an apprentice of the second landlord and cooks in the same stove as the defendant. If he is judged to be responsible for the disaster based solely on his words, it seems inappropriate. How could it be known that there were no other circumstances? Moreover, the price of yarn spools is not very cheap. Even if one wants to extract iron pieces, there is no need to use them as fuel. The judge ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and scheduled a date for sentencing.

Kidnappings Occur Frequently in Occupied Areas, One Bandit Executed by Firing Squad 88

In the towns and villages of Xinjing, Hongqiao, Qibao, and Changqiao in northwestern Shanghai, bandits are rampant and robberies are frequent since the area was occupied. Recently, they have become even more unscrupulous, daring to kidnap people for ransom in broad daylight. The puppet police generally turn a blind eye. Shen Zhigang, who lives in Caojiazhai, east of Beixinjing Town, was suddenly kidnapped by five bandits at around 9:00 a.m. the day before yesterday while Shen was in a tea house of a certain family in Beixinjing Town. Each bandit had a handgun. Shen was taken away and subjected to severe torture in the bandit's den. After half a month, his family managed to raise 800 yuan to redeem him and bring him home. Wang, the Ningbo owner of the Gong Sheng Weaving Factory in Gongjiazhai, north of Lincoln Road, was also kidnapped by bandits in broad daylight and demanded a ransom of 100,000 yuan. After several negotiations, he paid 16,000 yuan in foreign currency and was released the day before yesterday. Ding Shanming, the owner of the Yilong Rice Store in Hongqiao Town, was kidnapped in his store last month and has now been redeemed, but he still dares not return home. The old bookkeeper of the Yang Dingyuan Rice Store in Qibao Town's North Main Street was kidnapped with 7 staff members the night before last. It is heard that four of the old bookkeepers were released that night, but three staff members, including an employee Li, are still not out of danger. Shen Xiao Amei, a local who opened a cotton ginning factory in Changqiao Town on the Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe Road, was kidnapped by bandits the day before yesterday. His family paid 2,600 yuan in foreign currency to redeem him. Wang, the battalion commander of the 3rd regiment of the provincial security team, learned of the matter and arrested Kang Yinquan (former town mayor of Caojiaqiao from Guangang), one of the bandits involved. After interrogation, Wang determined that the confession was true. The day before yesterday, Kang was tied up and executed by firing squad in Changqiao Town. The remaining accomplices, Cai and others, are at large and are currently being hunted down.

Zhang Xuecheng, a native of Huzhou (24 years old), who is an apprentice at the Zhiyuan Transportation Company at No. 11 North Suzhou Road, is still unmarried. Recently, he has been fond of prostitution. At 4:00 p.m. on the 27th of last month, Wang Enpu, the manager of the company, gave him 350 yuan in legal tender, ordering him to send it to the Xixing Silk Store on Shanxi Road. Zhang, after obtaining the money, abandoned a receipt book in a wasteland and then went to prostitute himself at No. 49 West Zilaihuo Street in the French Concession with a prostitute named Hongbao, and at No. 9 Aiduya Road with a prostitute named Suzhen. He spent all the money in two weeks and avoided going to work at the company. Manager Wang Enpu negotiated with his guarantor surnamed Chen, and as a result, he paid 200 yuan in compensation. The afternoon before yesterday, at around 8:00 p.m., apprentice Zhang suddenly went to the transportation company to make a scene with Wang Enpu, wanting to get back the money compensated by the guarantor. Carrying Silver Ingots and Coins to Shanghai, Scoundrels Intercept and Extort, Police Investigate and Detain 90

Ji Yuanyu, a native of Suzhou, was recently instructed by Zhou Jintang, the owner of the Wansheng Silver Store on Manong Street in Suzhou, to bring ten raw silver ingots, weighing 200 taels, and 379 yuan in coins to Shanghai, intending to exchange them for legal tender at a certain money shop. At 10:00 a.m. the day before yesterday, while passing near the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Zha Pu Road, Wang Xinhai, a native of Yong who used to be a teacher at the Huaxing Primary School at No. 72 Tangshan Road, saw him,

stepped forward and stopped him

and asked about the source of the raw silver ingots and coins. While they were arguing, Wang Debiao, a Chinese detective from the Hongkou Public Security Bureau, and No. 433 Indian police saw them.

Teacher Wang immediately ran away, but was eventually caught. He was brought to the Public Security Bureau along with Ji Yuanyu's raw silver coins, silver ingots. Addicted to Gambling on Lotteries, Commits Suicide by Hanging 91

Yang Fubao, a native of Hangzhou, was 37 years old this year. He was unemployed and destitute, and was staying at the home of his friend, Yuan Guisheng, at No. 5 Beifu Lane, La Ge Na Road, French Concession. Because he was addicted to gambling on lotteries, and lost every time, resulting in a mountain of debt that he could not repay, he became despondent. Yesterday morning, he hanged himself on the iron railing of the drying platform stairs at Yuan's house. When his friend, Yuan Guisheng, got up and discovered him, he was already dead and beyond help. Dancer's Diamond Ring Stolen, Tenant Countersues for False Accusation 94

Yang Meili, a 22-year-old woman from Suzhou who used to be a dancer, living in the front building of No. 483 Fuxu Road, had a diamond ring hidden under her pillow on the bed stolen at noon on March 25th of the lunar calendar. Because Ma Zhao (47 years old), a fellow villager who lived in the back building, had come to her room to pick grass roots and was suspected, she reported it to the French Public Security Bureau. Ma Zhao was taken into custody for interrogation and detained for one night. Because there was no evidence of theft, she was released the next day. Now, Ma Zhao, whose husband is a prompter at the Great Stage, argued that she had been falsely accused of theft for no reason, which had affected her reputation, so she hired attorney Ling Xianlai to file a complaint with the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court, accusing Yang Meili of false accusation. Judge Miao Qingbang opened the court for trial the day before yesterday. The plaintiff and her lawyer appeared in court and stated the previous situation. The defendant, Yang Meili, testified that on that day, she and her sister were cooking downstairs, and there was no one in the room. The defendant came to my room to pick grass roots. When I went upstairs, the diamond ring was gone, so I reported it to the Public Security Bureau. When the detectives came to investigate, the defendant suddenly went out. After she came back, I went to the Public Security Bureau with her. My diamond ring was seen by everyone living in the same room, and everyone knew it was stolen. There was no false accusation. The court ordered the debate to end and scheduled a date for sentencing.

Assassin of Newspaper Vendor Leader Sentenced, Dissatisfied and Appeals, Waiting for Judgment 95

Wu Guisheng, the leader of newspaper vendors in Wangping Street, was assassinated by his colleagues at around 9:00 p.m. on March 21st of this year after leaving Runhua Hostel at No. 604 Fuzhou Road. The instigator, Little Bad Egg, is at large. Xu and others were sent to the First Special Court for interrogation. Xu Asi and others were dissatisfied with the judgment and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. Cao Bingsheng Dies in the Line of Duty, Special Compensation Given, and Gold Medal Awarded 97

After Inspector Cao Bingsheng of the Political Affairs Department of the French Concession Police Department was assassinated on the morning of the 6th of this month, the French police authorities and all people deeply mourned his death. The gunman, Wang Tingsheng (i.e. Wang Shiqing), was injured and captured at the scene. The truth of the case will be revealed after he recovers from his injuries. Regarding Cao's death in the line of duty, the issue of compensation for his family has been approved by the French Consul General after being submitted by the French Police Commissioner Fabre. In addition to the compensation of 3,000 yuan, a gold medal was specially awarded. The medal is engraved with the emblem of the French Concession to commend Cao's merits during his lifetime and to commemorate him forever. Cao is the first Chinese personnel in the French Police Department to receive this gold medal of honor. It is also heard that various groups and celebrities in the city will jointly initiate a memorial service, which is currently being prepared.

Buddhist Community Compiles and Prints a Grand Edition of the Avatamsaka Sutra 98

The Avatamsaka Sutra in Buddhism has a complete and wonderful meaning that surpasses everything. In the Tang Dynasty, the National Teacher Qingliang devoted his entire life's wisdom to writing a commentary on the Avatamsaka Sutra, elaborating on the meaning of the scripture, totaling sixty or seventy volumes. Its great value has always been revered by the Buddhist community. However, from the Song and Ming Dynasties to the Qing Dynasty, the transmission and engraving were corrupted, which was a major flaw. Recently, Elder Yingci and various lay Buddhists plan to recompile, collate, and reprint the book based on more than ten versions, in order to achieve the merit of receiving, upholding, lecturing, and reciting the scriptures, and to complete the incomplete classics of the past 1,300 years. A "Avatamsaka Sutra Commentary Compilation and Printing Association" was specially established at the Gongdelin Temple in this city on the 18th of this month, with the address at No. 712 Wei Hai Wei Road, specializing in this matter. The estimated printing cost is 20,000 yuan. Elder Yingci was publicly elected as the chairman, and Zhu Ziqiao, Ye Yufu, and Jiang Zhuzhuang were elected as the vice chairmen. Dharma Master Yuedong, Guan Jiongzhi, Shi Shengzhi, Fan Gunong, Li Qiqing, Li Yuanjing, Meng Wangqu, Ni Wenqing, Zhu Xiechen, Huang Youxi, and Fei Fanjiu were elected as permanent directors. Wen Lantian, Huang Hanzhi, Wu Yun, Ji Juemi, Nie Lingtai, Ding Zhonghu, Bao Cunwo, Wang Qiuhu, and Sheng Shengjiao were elected as directors, and prayed and made vows before the Buddha, resolving to complete the publication within three years. With this merit, they will dedicate it to all sentient beings in the world, eliminate karma, and bring about peace quickly. The printing fee of several thousand yuan has already been determined and deposited in the Jin Cheng Bank. In the future, payment will be made according to the book’s material costs, which is different from ordinary fundraising. The estimated price per book is 20 yuan, which will still be calculated according to the cost of the book at the time.

More Than Twenty Garbage Boats from the Two Concessions Detained in Southern Huangpu. Water Police Station Dispatches Japanese Personnel to Negotiate. Puppet "Water Police Team" Shrugs Off Responsibility 102

The garbage produced daily in the two special districts, the Public Concession and the French Concession, was transported by boats from the garbage wharf before the war, concentrated and dumped at the Longhua corner of the Southern Huangpu River. The old practice was continued after the war without hindrance. Unexpectedly, at 11:00 AM the day before yesterday, in the waters near Bailianjing (before reaching Longhua) in the Southern Huangpu, the puppet "Police Bureau Water Police Team" arbitrarily detained more than twenty garbage boats from the two concessions. It is reported that all the detained boats were fully loaded with garbage and had not yet reached their destination for dumping. In the afternoon of the same day, the Customs Water Police Station dispatched Japanese personnel to negotiate at the puppet "team" in Dongchang Road, Pudong. The puppet "Captain" Huo Liangchen evaded the responsibility by saying that he was acting on "orders from superiors," resulting in no results. The detained garbage boats had not been released as of yesterday afternoon.

Husband Hates Wife's Infidelity, Chops Injures Adulterers. Murderer Li Genlin Arrested. 103

Li Genlin, a native of Taizhou, a clerk at the Youxin Shoe Store on Xinzha Road, 25 years old, married Xu Xiuying, a woman from the same hometown (21 years old). Recently, due to the high cost of living, his wife was introduced to work as a maid in a Japanese family in Hongkou. She then developed an affair with Zhang Yongnian (28 years old), a fellow townsman who worked as a clerk in a Japanese store at No. 385 Wusong Road, Hongkou. After Li discovered this, he forced Xiuying to resign and return home. Not long after, Xiuying went to work as a maid in another Japanese home and continued her relationship with Zhang. Li, lacking a pass to Hongkou, could not go to Hongkou to negotiate, though he was filled with resentment. Until the night before last, Li learned that his wife and Zhang Yongnian had gone to the Haihualou Restaurant on North Zhejiang Road to attend a birthday banquet at a certain surname's house. Li secretly hid an axe and waited near the restaurant. At about 8:00 PM, when Xiuying and Zhang were walking out arm in arm after the banquet, Li immediately used the axe to chop at them several times. They fell to the ground wounded. Police officers rushed to the scene and summoned a car to send the woman to Guangren Hospital, while Zhang was sent to Baolong Hospital. The murderer Li Genlin has been arrested by the Huishi Police Station.

Apartment Owner Instigates Assault, Fined 104

Recently, Hu Shaochuan (37 years old, from Liyang), a former clerk of the Suzhou Wuxian Local Court, fled to Shanghai with his wife, Ms. Qian, due to the fall of Suzhou and the closure of the court. They resided in Room 219 of the Continental Apartment at No. 431 Rue Poupard (i.e. Datiebang), French Concession, paying a daily rent of one yuan. After living there for two months, they owed more than ten yuan in rent. On the night of March 14, the apartment manager, Xin Lichong from Ningbo, and the accountant, Xin Runquan, ordered a waiter to urge Hu to pay the rent. Due to a verbal conflict, Xin and others instigated Bai Yan, a clerk from the Hetaixing store in Room 103, to drag Hu out of his room and beat him violently. Hu's wife, Ms. Qian, stepped forward to dissuade them and was also beaten. The four-month-old child she was holding was also knocked to the ground, and developed a frightening sickness that led to his death. The Hu couple first filed a petition with the Special Second Court Procuratorate requesting a medical examination, and then hired lawyer Yao Yunbo to file a private prosecution for assault against Xin Lichong and Xin Runquan with the Criminal Division of the Special Second Court. Judge Liao Heng repeatedly opened court sessions for investigation, and summoned Le Wenchun, a resident of the Continental Apartment from Ningbo, to testify about the defendants' assault. The defendants admitted to instigating the assault and hired lawyers for their defense. The case was already concluded with the two defendants released on bail pending further review. This case has been concluded after interrogation and was adjudicated the day before yesterday. Xin Lichong was fined 400 yuan for instigating bodily harm, and Xin Runquan was fined 240 yuan for the same crime. It is reported that the defendants are dissatisfied with the verdict and are preparing to appeal to the High Third Branch Court.

Overview of the Work Report of the Animal Protection Society in March and April 105

The Shanghai Animal Protection Society reported in March and April of this year that countless people have called or come to the Society in person during these two months, requesting assistance in tracking down missing cats and dogs, entrusting the Society to find people to take in cats and dogs, or wanting to adopt cats and dogs. Although arranging for the accommodation of abandoned cats and dogs and pursuing missing cats and dogs can be regarded as a method of animal protection, most humanitarian societies do not regard it as within the scope of their activities. Therefore, there are small self-sufficient organizations specifically set up for this purpose, but no such organization exists in Shanghai. As a result, the Society's limited staff are extremely busy with this work, which takes up their time and energy to deal with more urgent matters.

Assistance and Protection Methods

Members of the public can provide great assistance to the Society in this matter by following the methods below: (1) Implement various preventive measures to avoid cats and dogs from getting lost or being stolen, such as instructing servants to close the doors of gardens and residences and pay attention to the integrity of garden fences; (2) When servants walk dogs, they must be instructed to leash the dog by the neck and take it for a walk, allowing it to walk on crowded streets; (3) The dog's license plate must always be attached to the collar, and the collar must always be worn, so that even if the dog is lost, there is a license number to check to find its owner; (4) Those who want to adopt cats and dogs can go directly to the dog houses of the French Concession or the Public Concession工部局to select them, without having to contact the Society first; (5) Join the Society as a member and pay membership fees or donate funds to expand the number of staff to cope with this matter.

General Abuse of Animals

The worst case of abuse in this period was found in the Caojiabo slaughterhouse outside the concession, where pigs, horses and cattle were inhumanely slaughtered, either chopped with axes or hoes, or allowed to bleed to death slowly. These abuse incidents have been published in newspapers and the March issue of the Blue Cross Magazine (the Society's quarterly). It is known that many horses abandoned after the races are sold and enter this slaughterhouse from the stables to suffer a terrible death. Therefore, the Society has appealed to racehorse owners to humanely destroy lame and unsuitable horses, and prevent them from participating in auctions. The Society is now taking possible steps to remedy the situation in this slaughterhouse, but due to its location outside the concession, it is difficult to take strict action. At present, the Society is working to prevent horses from being sent to this terrible slaughterhouse.

When the investigator last inspected the slaughterhouse, he saw a water buffalo lying on the ground, its limbs tied to wooden pillars, its head tied to an iron ring on the ground, and a two-inch diameter wound cut in its neck, allowing it to bleed to death.

On March 7, a member of the Society reported seeing a lame horse being dragged along Daxilu. After investigation, it was found that the horse was being taken by a groom to the above-mentioned slaughterhouse to suffer a terrible death. The Society immediately visited the horse owner and arranged for the horse to be humanely destroyed. The horse's body was then removed by strangers. On one of the hottest days in April, it was reported that two calves had collapsed on Jiangxi Road. The Society's ambulance immediately transported them to their destination. The owner was fined ten yuan by the French Concession authorities.

Investigators have repeatedly discovered the live plucking of pig bristles. One case was prosecuted in court, and the offender was sentenced to ten days in jail for theft.

He was sent to Guangci Hospital for treatment, and the medical expenses were borne by this shop. Later, Xuesheng's brother, Ahe, moved Xuesheng from Guangci Hospital to Lixing Inn on Wuhu Road, and this shop continued to bear the medical expenses. Then Ahe carried Xuesheng to this shop. How the inn refused to accept him, and how the police were reported, are all unknown to me. Moreover, Jue Sunshunsheng is too young and does not participate in shop affairs. Last year, Zhao Ahe asked Qian, a lawyer, to send a letter to ask for a settlement. I knew his purpose and ignored it. This time, he has requested an additional 9,900 yuan in civil litigation, and part of the statement remains reserved for a subsequent request. It has come to the time when the dagger is revealed. Free Talk

A Message to Young Literary People with New Hobbies 111

— Shangqing

When addressing young literary people with old hobbies, my first sentence was: it is best if you do not indulge in literary hobbies. Now, when addressing young literary people with new hobbies, the first thing I want to say is still: it is best if you do not indulge in literary hobbies. The reason has been mentioned before, so I won't repeat it here.

Unfortunately, there are quite a few young people who are fond of old literature, and even more young people who are fond of new literature. Therefore, as a second-best option, I can only use my sincere wishes to tell young people who are fond of new literature a few words:

If you are truly fond of new literature, and you want to appreciate, study, or create it, but you don't know where to start, I suggest you start with Western literature. The establishment of our new literature can be said to be entirely influenced by Western literature. Almost all famous new literary writers are proficient in Western languages and literature. They started with Western literature, so they laid the foundation for our new literature today. However, our new literature today is still far from being fully developed and capable of enlightening future generations. We still need to work hard on the same path, and the most fundamental way is still to first understand Western literature.

To understand Western literature, it is best to be able to understand the language of a certain Western country so that you can read directly. Otherwise, reading many translated works is also a good way. Translated works with good writing and content are of course the most suitable for us. Even if the writing is not very good, as long as the content is not bad, we can still extract its essence and focus on the spirit rather than the form.

After you have read a lot of Western literature, know what the spirit of new literature is, what the differences between new literature and old literature are, and you have thoroughly understood the general technical points, then you will naturally want to start writing. Perhaps at this time you will have another question: what kind of writing should I use to write well? Or, to what extent should I write to be considered good?

There is a lot of room for flexibility in the level of "good," so I cannot set a standard or define what constitutes "good." However, I can say what the minimum level of "good" should be, and that is: it must be coherent. Sentences should not have grammatical errors; paragraphs should not have ambiguous flaws; the structure should not be too rigid or too chaotic; the intention should not be profound but not easily understood.

Of course, everyone wants to be coherent; but how can one achieve coherence? Perhaps this is the question that will ultimately arise.

To solve this problem: first, you still need to study Western literature; second, you need to study high-quality new literary works. Western literature is generally coherent, but since the writing is different, it cannot directly help our writing, so we still have to study our existing high-quality literary works. By "high-quality," I don't mean to point them out one by one. Generally speaking, new literary books published by the Commercial Press, the Chung Hwa Book Company, the World Book Company, and the Kaiming Bookstore can all be considered high-quality. Of course, there may also be high-quality new literary books published by other bookstores, but there are also some inferior ones, so you need to be selective.

I strongly disapprove of the idea that in order to create new literature, one must study old literature, as if reviewing the old can really lead to new understanding. I would rather see Europeanized sentences with awkward usage of "na ne ma" than see fluent classical Chinese clichés using "zhi hu zhe ye," because the former is easy to improve, while the latter is a deeply ingrained habit that is almost incurable. Of course, today's new literary writers did not succeed simply by studying Western literature and completely abandoning old literature. Old literature can indeed contribute to new literature. However, I believe that studying old literature always has more disadvantages than advantages. To avoid confusing people, it is best not to consult old literature.

I dare not say that the current literary supplements in newspapers and various magazines have reached a good level in terms of writing, so we don't need to emulate them. However, incoherent literature does appear in supplements or magazines, which is a fact. Because supplements and magazines have time constraints, they inevitably have oversights, unlike single-volume books, which can be carefully polished and strive for perfection. Therefore, I hope that those who want to study new literature from supplements or magazines to improve their own new literary writing should be very careful. As for some deliberately superficial writing with ulterior motives, I think you shouldn't learn it at all.

When you have a complete grasp of the content and form of new literature, you can naturally start writing freely. But when you create, I still want to tell you two things:

Do not use your talent to engage in destructive work. Sarcasm and ridicule are sometimes necessary, but you shouldn't think that it is the only skill a writer should have. The garden of literature is vast, and the flowers and fruits in it are definitely not just cursing or ridiculing people. As for cursing wrongly or unreasonably, that is of course not allowed. Why have writers been looked down upon throughout history and called "frivolous"? This tradition of excluding dissenters is also a major reason! Similarly, self-promotion, mutual flattery, and self-congratulation are also undesirable, as their only effect is to destroy literature and misuse your talent. I hope you can also avoid these.

Do not write articles solely for yourself, especially not in the current era. "Art for art's sake" may be acceptable in prosperous times, but now, if you have the talent for writing, you should only dedicate it to the country and the nation. At the very least, even if you want to sigh and complain, you should look at those who are more unfortunate than you and sigh and complain on their behalf, because you have a pen and don't have to worry about opportunities, while they have nothing. If you don't help them, no one will. Therefore, I hope you use fewer trivial matters around you as material. The above are my words to young literary people with new hobbies. Of course, this is just my personal limited view, and there are many places that need to be supplemented or discussed further. Due to space limitations, I can only leave it at that for now.

General Lu 112

— Shengdan

— War Zone Notes

After Lao Tai went to Ruichang with the army, Jianxiong had to leave for Xianning soon because his vacation was over, and I, having arrived in Hankou from Lu'an, had to return to the Dabie Mountains to continue the work I was supposed to do. At this time, the battle around Wu'ao had entered a critical stage, but because I had arranged to meet General Lu Han, I had to delay my departure to see the demeanor of the famous Yunnan army general. Moreover, he had made special contributions in the Battle of Taierzhuang, and I felt it was necessary to meet him in order to collect some valuable historical materials. So, although I was ready to leave, I did not immediately say goodbye to Wuhan. At the same time, the defense area he was in charge of this time happened to be at the end of the Yuehan Railway in Hunan Province. If the Three Towns were to be swallowed up, then he would bear a great responsibility in the western Hubei area. Therefore, my departure date for returning to the Dabie Mountains was extended by two weeks.

I remember it was a day of very heavy air raids. Several more deep pools were added to the Hanyang Airport. Fortunately, the soil was unlucky and flew around for no reason. They always use the things they get from "taxing the people to the fullest" to fight with the soil, which really feels like a waste. Therefore, friends who came back from the war zone all showed an indifferent attitude towards bombings. After the air raid alarm was lifted, the phone rang: "General Lu is waiting for you at Dingyuli in Hunan Street. Please come immediately. He is going to cross the river this afternoon!" It was Director Peng of the Political Training Department speaking, with a heavy Yunnan accent.

When I arrived at Dingyuli, the first people I saw were several young girls from the Yunnan Women's War Zone Work Team. During my previous visit, I had become quite familiar with them. But what gift did I have? None at all; all I had was a respectful greeting.

When I met General Lu, his "gentle and refined" demeanor made me wonder if he was a scholar, or perhaps a university professor? His orderly conversation was like that of a "eloquent" diplomat. He talked about their breakout from Xuzhou and the long journey of over seven hundred li on foot, without any fatigue, just like the female students from Anhui University's War Zone Work Team that I saw in Huayang, full of energy. "Santa Claus is here, you must have brought some gifts!" The girls really knew how to joke. My conversation with them lasted for two hours before it finally stopped. The topic, of course, was the past Battle of Taierzhuang. Finally, he said, "When we triumph in the future, let's meet at the Yellow Crane Tower!"

With a sincere smile, I shook hands with General Lu and said goodbye.

Light is Already in Sight 113

— Liu Zenghui

Plea 114

— Qian Changnian

It is not a low groan, nor is it a wind-like wail, but the tears of our millions of people, flowing into a sea, and from this sea comes a sound like a giant wave. These millions of suffering hearts of ours—perhaps the most unfortunate. Those whose fates are governed by different fortunes never think of these hearts that have only suffered. Who knows the deep pain sometimes inflicted upon our hearts, making us forget that our bodies are also wandering helplessly? Who gives us the friendship of love? That is a dream! They ultimately have their own fortunes, sometimes casting a glance of sincere sympathy upon us for a moment, but after turning their heads, they love their own fortunes even more deeply. To whom can we turn to plead? Truth has hidden itself in the deep valleys, having long forgotten this group of us!

We are forced to act out tragedies. Will truth give us a bit of light? There must be a ray of light in the darkness. As long as it can give us a bit of hope, we can go and seek it.

Why have our homes become piles of rubble? We did not excessively enjoy ourselves in them. Why has shapeless flesh and blood stained our rice fields? Why has our beloved child been taken away, he will no longer cry for milk when he is hungry, no longer intimately snuggle in my arms and shout "fear?" Why must tears drip onto my own severed arm that I am tightly holding?

Truth, please illuminate this world again, do not lightly abandon this group of countless suffering people. Give us a ray of hope!

Wandering aimlessly, without a home, a wandering that seems to have no seasons, when the fierce summer sun mercilessly shines down, sweat soaking through our ragged clothes that never dry. There are also big houses there, but we dare not set foot inside, because they do not need truth. The days slip away like this forever, the seasons are not kind to us. The biting cold wind wraps around our bodies in the harsh winter, and we still wear the same torn clothes we wore in the summer. Although our bodies are frozen, there is still a conscious heart that has not frozen to death, and this heart is forever marked with a question—'Is this the verdict of truth?'

Heaven! This is not a curse, because perhaps this is fate. Looking at that bright and warm place, but we do not have the courage to knock on the door. Who would bother to listen to our lament? Which door would accommodate us, these homeless wanderers? Even if the wind blows down this body that cannot withstand hunger and cold, in the eyes of others, it may be no more than a dog that has frozen to death!

Who has ever witnessed the blood of their own aged parents staining a sharp blade? Lying in the rubble, groaning in pain? Their hearts were just as loving towards their children as other people's parents, but they encountered a situation contrary to reason and compassion. They never complained that their children were not as good as others, but in their hearts at the moment of eternal farewell, they still held a thought, deeply fearing that their children suffering on this bloody ground would encounter even more cruel devastation!

Whenever we pray for the coming of truth, we feel something stuck in our throats, as if the blood in our hearts is dripping down. Our deep voices turn into trembling sobs. What more suffering awaits us? Yet we do not expect to die. Perhaps when we reach the end of suffering, we will finally be saved. Enduring the pain, harboring this hope: behind the layers of dark clouds hides the sun, and darkness will eventually be driven out of the world!

Learning to Cry 115

— Gu Chu

It seems someone once said, "Crying is a sign of weakness." Yes, when two children fight, the weaker one will inevitably lose, and when they lose, they will inevitably cry. From this, we can also prove that "crying is a sign of weakness" is correct, so why should we "learn" it?

However, clever people say: crying is a method of being human, a secret to success. Their reasoning is that "everyone has a heart of compassion," and the way to touch other people's compassion is to "cry." They also cite a large number of successful people, like Liu Xuande, like Shen Baoxu, like...etc., to prove that "crying" is the secret to success. Since "crying" is the secret to success, its importance is obvious, and how can one not "learn" it? But how to learn? And how to "put it to use" after learning? Let's give some examples to clarify:

For example: You see that the hearts of people in society are not as they used to be, and the social atmosphere is deteriorating. So you give a speech in public on the methods to remedy this, but you must shed a few tears; or publish an article, but in the article, you must not omit the words "alas"—or, to be more Westernized, use "oh"—then people will be moved and give you the title of "moralist." When you encounter refugees on the street asking you for money, you can turn your head and walk away—the faster you walk, the better; but when you return to your mansion, you must "ping ping ze ze" write a few ancient or modern poems of "mourning the refugees" or "crying for fellow compatriots," and use a classic quote such as "Behind vermilion gates, meat and wine go to waste, while on the road lie the bones of those who have starved to death," and publish it in a newspaper or magazine. Then people will call you a "poet elder" and give you the title of "philanthropist." If your parents or other elders in your family die, you can watch movies or hold dancing girls, but the most important thing is that in the "obituary" or "announcement of mourning," you must not omit the words "weeping blood" or "shedding tears," even if you feel no pain in your heart. But when you meet friends, your eyes must be as red as blood, and when you speak, your voice must be slightly trembling. Then people will still say that you are able to "grieve to the point of emaciation" and crown you with the title of "filial son." Similarly, when talking about national affairs, you must cry bitterly, or sob uncontrollably, to show that your "love for the country does not lag behind others." Therefore, people will still crown you with the title of "patriot"...

If you don't want titles, then is there no place to use crying? Well, there are other uses.

For example: If you want to borrow money from someone, you must wear a mournful face (if you can really cry, that's even better, but if you can't, at least show some crying expression), then people will believe that you really have no money and are truly poor. Otherwise, you will definitely be turned away and hit a wall. If you fail a class in school, you just need to go to the teacher and wail loudly, preferably with tears streaming down your face, explaining the reasons why you failed. Then you can pass and be promoted. If you quarrel with your husband, or fight and suffer losses, then you just need to "cry," "cry" at the ancestral altar, for an hour, two hours, a day, two days...then your husband will definitely be impressed and fall at your feet under your short cheongsam, obeying your every command.

Since the way of crying came into being, it has spread from one to ten, ten to a hundred, and everyone is vying to emulate it, each using their ingenuity, creating a chilling and ghostly atmosphere. Therefore, I picked up my pen and judged:

"The way of being a human lies in deception, the way of deception lies in crying. The clever people do not die, and the chaos does not stop!"

Spring and Autumn

Outdoor Summer Concerts Organized by the Shanghai Municipal Council Music Band 116

— Zhang Zhenshan

Starting June 1st and Ending August 31st, Stages and Seats are Being Actively Arranged in Various Parks

The early summer monsoon brings information about the summer heat, covering the city with a summer coat, making all life's movements flow into the summer rapids. Cold drinks and swimming pools have begun to become active; all moving and still things are changing regularly with the shift of seasons.

The outdoor summer concerts organized annually by the Shanghai Municipal Council Music Band are now ready and will begin playing on June 1st ahead of schedule. Originally, it was customary to start on July 1st and end at the end of September. Starting a month earlier this year, this correction of the time arrangement is indeed very appropriate, because the number of visitors to the park in June is gradually increasing, while the number of park visitors in September is decreasing.

It is not yet the hottest day, and the parks in France, Béthune Park, Zhao Feng Park, the Bund Park, and Jiaozhou Park are already extremely crowded, especially the crowds wandering around in the afternoon. If we calculate the ratio of the five million citizens to the area of these few parks, it is indeed not enough. Therefore, in the "isolated island," in the season when people need to let out some heat, as long as there is some artificially decorated greenery, there will inevitably be a phenomenon of being full to the brim. It seems that open-air concerts can be held in any park this summer, but because of the equipment and location, there are only four locations where they can be played: Zhao Feng Park, the Bund Park, France Park, and the French Association. But France Park and the French Association are only separated by a low wall, so in fact, there are only three locations. Now it is stipulated that from June 1, brass music will be played every Wednesday and Thursday in France Park; every Friday in the Bund Park; and every Tuesday and Saturday in Zhao Feng Park.

Starting June 14, in addition to the above brass concerts as usual, orchestral music will also be played from 9:00 PM to 11:00 PM at the following two locations:—every Thursday at the French Association; every Monday and Saturday at Zhao Feng Park.

The park bureaus are now actively arranging and scrubbing the performance stage and seats. Except that Zhao Feng Park has a ready-made semi-circular bandstand, and the Bund Park also has a ready-made hexagonal pavilion, the performance stage in France Park is temporarily built with foreign pine wood planks under the large trees in the middle of the park; the performance stage of the French Association is to use the original terrace in front of the building, covered with blue cloth.

When the open-air concerts are played, in addition to the park tickets, you also need to buy additional tickets. Tickets for orchestral concerts are divided into two types: one yuan and fifty cents; brass concerts do not sell tickets, but rent for canvas lounge chairs, charging twenty cents per person.

Based on past situations and experience, because most of the music played is famous songs from European and Western countries, most Chinese people, except for a small number who have researched music art, do not understand the kind of rhythm, music theory, nature, origin of the music, literary value, and the technology of its performance. They only use its sound to regulate the monotony and loneliness of their hearing. The so-called artistic and poetic appreciation has not yet become universal and popular, so the audience is not as crowded as for low-level song and dance, and even rows of lounge chairs are empty, which is equivalent to being set up in vain. From this, we can see the general public's degree of appreciation for musical art.

However, on the other hand, in terms of the principle of saving consumption, it is advisable to listen while sitting on the grass without spending money, because the sound is no different from listening while lying on a chair, and you do not have to be restricted by your position, you can move freely. Moreover, it is not necessary to spend money to be considered to understand musical art! As long as you have free time, you can listen to your heart's content every afternoon or evening within two months without spending any money!

A Note on the Aurora Museum 117

— Lanyan

With Various Insect Hatching Processes and Specimens of Colorful Butterflies, it is the Crystallization of French Priests' Efforts

The intellectual classes, who are buried in a world of eroticism, rarely visit museums or other places for academic research. To put it bluntly, how many people can often go to the library to smell the scent of books?

Someone said that Chinese science is not progressing. I say that at the very least, we must change the living environment of Shanghai people.

Regarding museums, I know that there are two in total in the Shanghai concessions, one is the museum on Museum Road, and the other is the museum attached to Aurora University.

Before the Shanghai War, the Shanghai Municipal Government spent a lot of money to build a museum, and held an exhibition of architectural styles of past dynasties, with detailed explanations and introductions to the greatness of ancient buildings.

Now, this museum is buried in smoke and rubble, which is indeed a source of endless vicissitudes.

Regarding the Aurora Museum, I had broken the rules and visited it once before it was open. The day before yesterday, they held their 70th anniversary ceremony, and the various specimens collected were particularly rich.

Now, I will write down a little bit of material that has not been recorded in the various newspapers:

From this 70-year-old Aurora Museum, we can also see that the energy that religious scholars have put into China is indeed amazing. Starting with the founder, Father Heude, and continuing through Fathers Le Doré, Père Heude, Père Blanc, Père Sicard, to the current person in charge, Father Zheng, they have worked tirelessly and continuously, overcoming many hardships and struggles, to collect so many valuable specimens.

These many priests specialize in collecting one or two types of specimens. For example, Father Le Doré's collection of deer specimens is the richest in the Far East (now there are a total of 3,675 types); the founder, Father Heude, traveled around the earth almost seven times in order to collect various specimens; and now, he has left China with many precious "Chinese Natural History" works. These works have made great contributions to those who study natural science in China. There is also Father Blanc, who specializes in the study of plants, and Father Sicard, who specializes in collecting insects.

The entire museum has three floors. The bottom floor is for antiques and bronzes, which I visited before; the second floor is for plant specimens and animal specimens; and the third floor is for insect, shell, and bird specimens.

Among the insect specimens, there are many various kinds of insects and ants that you have never seen before, and the processes of how they live and hatch. For example, a small bamboo tube is the perfect place for a small insect to hatch; a piece of soil is the perfect home for another type of insect. These specimens are all living, step by step showing their nests and changes.

In particular, many colorful butterfly specimens are really extremely beautiful. These insects, which represent the colors of nature, are worth lingering over.

Among the birds, there are even more exquisite specimens, such as a tiny bird, how it arranges its nest in a branch and a bamboo tube, and how it hatches its eggs.

After visiting this Aurora Museum, which includes hundreds of thousands of specimens of animals, plants, and insects, people feel the greatness and beauty of nature even more.

This museum is open to the public for two weeks starting yesterday. After two weeks, there may be a small fee to enter.

Now that such an opportunity exists, of course, I cannot let it pass lightly. I am very gratified, thinking that my long-cherished wish of several years can be fulfilled. However, the early hour gives me pause. Shops in Shanghai generally open around 7:00 AM and close at 9:00 PM. If I were to ask the shop owner for leave to attend school every day before 9:00 PM, it would be quite impossible. With best wishes for your well-being.

After the Rain, Clear Skies 120

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Ten: Simple Hairdo and Blue Skirt, a Virtuous and Good Mother; White Beard and Emerald Sleeves, a Vigorous Old Man

He Liyu asked, "Is that Mrs. Xu, the village chief, right now?" Village Chief Zhu said, "Isn't it? Later on, this old man and young woman actually formed this couple. So, before Old Man Xu's family property was completely dissipated, people thought that Xie Ayu's marriage to him was to covet his property. After the old man died, she could sweep away everything and leave. Even if Xie Ayu didn't have this intention, people would often suspect her.
